  <!-- 
	This box a cloned search box for  Market Indices boxes (on homepage, market page & some charts pages)
	The reason of making a clone is because the content after the search box cannot be loaded if barchart's search box
	is not loaded. So we put the below code at the end of the page and copy the script to the symbol_search_form_container
	once the page is fully loaded
-->
  <div id="search_box_clone" style="display:none;">
   <script src="//kitco2.websol.barchart.com/?module=basicSearchForm&amp;js=1&amp;popup=1" type="text/javascript">
   </script>
  </div>
  <script>
   document.getElementById ('symbol_search_form_container').innerHTML = document.getElementById ('search_box_clone').innerHTML;
	document.getElementById ('search_box_clone').innerHTML = "";
	var sym_search_input = document.getElementById('ac-input');
	if ( sym_search_input != null ) 
	{
		sym_search_input.placeholder = "Symbol or name";
	}
  </script>

  <script>
   (function() {
			$('#homepage_feedback_form input[type=submit]').on('click', function(e) {
				if ($('#homepage_feedback_form textarea').val().length > 1) {
					fLoc = '/scripts/survey/main_comments.pl?type=17&comment=' + escape(document.feedback.comment.value);
					fPopUp = window.open(fLoc, 'FeedbackThankYou', 'top=50,left=200,width=300,height=200,channelmode=0,dependant=1,fullscreen=0,resizable=no,toolbar=0,status=0,scrollbars=1,location=0,menubar=0,directories=0');
				} else {
					e.preventDefault();
					alert('Please enter your feedback message.');
				}
			});

			});

  <script type="text/javascript">
   (function() {
			var getShanghai = function(el) {
				var date = (new Date('Mar 18, 2021'));
				var month = date.getMonth() + 1;
				var day = date.getDate();
				var year = date.getFullYear();

				if (month.toString().length === 1) { month = '0' + month; } else { month; }
				if (day.toString().length === 1) { day = '0' + day; } else { day; }

				var dateReq = year + '-' + month + '-' + day;

				var currency = $(el + ' .select_container').eq(0).find('#shf-currency-select li[rel="' + Cookies.get('SHIndex_currency')  + '"]').html();
				$(el + ' .select_container').eq(0).find('.selected').attr('rel',  Cookies.get('SHIndex_currency'));
				$(el + ' .select_container').eq(0).find('.selected').html(currency);
				$(el + ' .select_container').eq(1).find('select').val(Cookies.get('SHIndex_unit'));

				currency = $(el + ' .select_container').eq(0).find('.selected').attr('rel');
				var unit = $(el + ' .select_container').eq(1).find('select').val();

				// ajax call
				var getPrices = function(currency, dateReq, unit) {
					$.ajax({
						method: 'GET',
						url: '//proxy.kitco.com/getshidx?currency=' + currency + '&df=1&date=' + dateReq,
						dataType: 'text',
						beforeSend: function() {
							$(el + ' #shf-data #shf-am #shf-am-value').text('-');
							$(el + ' #shf-data #shf-pm #shf-pm-value').text('-');
						}
					}).done(function(data) {
						var res = data.split(',');
						var am = res[2];
						var pm = res[3];

						$(el + ' #shf-data #shf-am #shf-am-value').text(convertPriceByUnit(am, unit));
						$(el + ' #shf-data #shf-pm #shf-pm-value').text(convertPriceByUnit(pm, unit));
					}).fail(function() {
						$(el + ' #shf-data #shf-am #shf-am-value').text('NA');
						$(el + ' #shf-data #shf-pm #shf-pm-value').text('NA');
					});
				}

				getPrices(currency, dateReq, unit);

				$(el + ' .select_container').eq(0).on('click', function(e) {
					var _this = $(this);
					var options = _this.children().children('ul').children('li');

					options.on('click', function() {
						var _this = $(this);
						var rel = _this.attr('rel');
						Cookies.set('SHIndex_currency', rel);
						var content = $(_this.prop('tagName') + '[rel=' + rel + ']').html();
						var currency = rel;
						var unit = _this.parent().parent().parent().siblings('.select_container').children().find('select').val();

						// ajax call
						getPrices(currency, dateReq, unit);

						_this.parent().siblings('.selected').html(content);
						_this.parent().siblings('.selected').attr('rel', rel);
						_this.parent().hide();
					});
				});

				$(el + ' .select_container').eq(1).on('click', function(e) {
					var _this = $(this);
					var select = _this.children().children('select');
					var options = _this.children().children('select').children('option');

					select.on('change', function() {
						var _this = $(this);
						var value = _this.val();
						var currency = _this.parent().parent().siblings('.select_container').find('.selected').attr('rel');
						var unit = value;

						// ajax call
						getPrices(currency, dateReq, unit);
					});
				});

				$(el + ' #shf-date').datepick({
					onSelect: function(dates) {
						var _this = $(this);
						var date = dates;
						var month, day;
						date = date[0];
						date = new Date(date);
						var month = date.getMonth() + 1;
						var day = date.getDate();
						var year = date.getFullYear();

						if (date[0].toString().length === 1) { month = '0' + date[0]; } else { month = date[0] }
						if (date[1].toString().length === 1) { day = '0' + date[1]; } else { day = date[1] }

						dateReq = year + '-' + month + '-' + day;
						var currency = _this.siblings('.select_container').eq(0).children().find('.selected').attr('rel');
						var unit = _this.siblings('.select_container').eq(1).children().children().val();

						// ajax call
						getPrices(currency, dateReq, unit);
					},
					minDate:'Apr 19, 2016',
					maxDate:'Mar 18, 2021',
					defaultDate: '0',
					selectDefaultDate: true,
					showTrigger: '#calImg',
					dateFormat: 'M dd, yyyy'
				});
			};

			getShanghai('.mobile-shanghai');
			getShanghai('.desktop-shanghai');
		})();
  </script>
